## Unit 48 — Saber: Aspectual Shift — soube vs sabia

*Slug: `b1-saber-aspect-bp` · Sequence position: 46.6 · CEFR: B1 · Variant: bp*

**Concepts:** `aspectual-shift-saber`

**Prereqs:** `a2-pret-poder-querer-saber`, `a2-imp-regular`, `a2-pret-vs-imp`, `a2-saber-vs-conhecer`

### Outcomes

- Distinguish **soube** (found out, learned at a specific moment) from **sabia** (knew, was already aware)
- Use temporal markers (ontem, sempre, quando, há anos) to signal which reading is intended
- Recognize that English "I knew" maps to either form depending on context

### Vocabulary

Triggering markers for **soube** (inception of knowledge):
- ontem, na semana passada, no mês passado
- quando + [event] (at the moment of...)
- só / finalmente (only then / finally)
- pelos jornais, pela Maria (through, from)

Triggering markers for **sabia** (state of knowledge):
- sempre, desde criança, desde sempre
- naquela época, quando era criança
- já (already, in the sense of "had known for a while")

### Grammar

The same verb shifts meaning by tense:

- **soube** = found out, learned, discovered → marks the moment knowledge was acquired
- **sabia** = knew → describes ongoing knowledge, with no inception event in focus

### Exemplar pairs

- *Eu **soube** ontem que ela está grávida.* — I found out yesterday that she's pregnant.
- *Eu **sabia** que ela estava grávida.* — I knew she was pregnant. (already knew)

- *Só **soube** do problema quando você me contou.* — I only found out about the problem when you told me.
- *Eu **sabia** do problema, mas não falei nada.* — I knew about the problem, but didn't say anything.

- *Quando você **soube** da notícia?* — When did you find out about the news?
- *Você **sabia** que ele mora aqui?* — Did you know he lives here?

- *Quando eu era criança, eu já **sabia** ler.* — When I was a child, I already knew how to read.

### Drills & artifacts

<!-- TODO: link existing pretérito vs imperfeito drills; consider authoring a saber-specific drill in /drill-create. -->

### Traps

- **English "I knew" is ambiguous.** Default-translating it to *eu sabia* is usually safe, but if the context is "I found out" (a moment of discovery), the correct form is *soube*. Listen for "when did you find out" → *quando você soube?*, not *quando você sabia?*
- **Time markers are the strongest disambiguator.** *Ontem*, *no mês passado*, *quando me contou* all push toward *soube*. *Sempre*, *desde*, *já* push toward *sabia*.
- The negation flips: *não sabia* = didn't know (state). *Não soube* = didn't find out, never learned about it.

---

## Unit 49 — Conhecer: Aspectual Shift — conheci vs conhecia

*Slug: `b1-conhecer-aspect-bp` · Sequence position: 46.7 · CEFR: B1 · Variant: bp*

**Concepts:** `aspectual-shift-conhecer`

**Prereqs:** `a2-pret-regular-er-ir`, `a2-imp-regular`, `a2-pret-vs-imp`, `a2-saber-vs-conhecer`

### Outcomes

- Distinguish **conheci** (met for the first time / went to a place for the first time) from **conhecia** (was acquainted with, was familiar with)
- Use this pair fluently in life-story narration and travel talk
- Recognize that English "I met" almost always maps to *conheci*, while "I knew" maps to *conhecia*

### Vocabulary

Triggering markers for **conheci** (first encounter, first visit):
- ontem, no ano passado, em [year]
- numa festa, no trabalho, na faculdade (where you met)
- Verb often paired with the question: *Como vocês se conheceram?*

Triggering markers for **conhecia** (familiarity, prior acquaintance):
- há anos, desde criança, há muito tempo
- já (already, in the sense of "had known for a while")
- naquela época, antes de

### Grammar

- **conheci** = met (a person for the first time) / visited (a place for the first time) → punctual event of acquaintance
- **conhecia** = knew, was familiar with → ongoing acquaintance with no first-meeting event in focus

### Exemplar pairs

- *Eu **conheci** o Pedro numa festa, em 2020.* — I met Pedro at a party, in 2020.
- *Eu **conhecia** o Pedro há anos antes de ele se mudar.* — I'd known Pedro for years before he moved.

- *Quando você **conheceu** seu marido?* — When did you meet your husband?
- *Eu **conhecia** o seu marido só de vista.* — I knew your husband only by sight.

- *Eu **conheci** São Paulo na viagem do ano passado.* — I went to São Paulo for the first time on last year's trip.
- *Eu **conhecia** São Paulo bem na época em que morava lá.* — I knew São Paulo well back when I lived there.

- *Você já **conhece** o restaurante novo?* — Have you been to the new restaurant?
- *Eu não **conhecia** esse autor antes.* — I wasn't familiar with this author before.

### Drills & artifacts

<!-- TODO: pair with the (placeholder) a2-saber-vs-conhecer unit and any existing pret/imp drills. -->

### Traps

- **English "I met" maps to conheci, never to conhecia.** *Eu o conhecia em 2020* is wrong — it should be *Eu o conheci em 2020*.
- **English "I knew him/her" almost always maps to conhecia** (familiarity). *Eu o conheci há anos* would mean "I met him years ago" (the meeting event), not "I had known him for years."
- *Conhecer* applied to a place takes the first-visit reading in *conheci*. *Eu conheci Lisboa* = I visited Lisbon for the first time, not "I knew Lisbon."
- *Já conhece?* in BP is a polite "Have you been there before?" / "Are you already familiar with it?" — present tense carries the perfect-aspect reading.

---

## Unit 50 — Poder: Aspectual Shift — pude vs podia

*Slug: `b1-poder-aspect-bp` · Sequence position: 46.8 · CEFR: B1 · Variant: bp*

**Concepts:** `aspectual-shift-poder`

**Prereqs:** `a2-pret-poder-querer-saber`, `a2-imp-regular`, `a2-pret-vs-imp`

### Outcomes

- Distinguish **pude** (managed to, succeeded in doing on a specific occasion) from **podia** (was able to, had the general ability or context)
- Express past attempts and accomplishments precisely
- Recognize that English "I could" is ambiguous and forces a context-driven choice

### Vocabulary

Triggering markers for **pude** (specific accomplishment):
- ontem, finalmente, depois de muito esforço
- só / apenas (only then)
- conseguir + infinitivo (often paraphrasable as *consegui* — same aspect)
- Negative: *não pude* = didn't manage to / wasn't able to (this time)

Triggering markers for **podia** (general ability or background context):
- sempre, quando era jovem, naquela época
- antigamente, no meu tempo
- background descriptions of what was possible (often paired with another past tense)

### Grammar

- **pude** = managed to / succeeded in → completed action, specific moment, often after effort
- **podia** = was able to / had the ability → ongoing capacity, context, no specific outcome in focus

### Exemplar pairs

- *Finalmente **pude** terminar o relatório.* — I finally managed to finish the report.
- *Quando eu era jovem, **podia** correr 10 km sem parar.* — When I was young, I could run 10 km without stopping.

- *Não **pude** ir à festa, tive que trabalhar.* — I couldn't make it to the party, I had to work. (specific occasion)
- *Naquela época, eu não **podia** sair sozinho.* — Back then, I wasn't allowed to go out alone. (ongoing context)

- *Só ontem **pude** falar com ele.* — Only yesterday did I manage to talk to him.
- *Eu **podia** falar com ele sempre que quisesse.* — I could talk to him whenever I wanted. (general access)

- *Você **pôde** ver o jogo?* — Were you able to catch the game? (this time)
- *No domingo eu sempre **podia** ver o jogo.* — On Sundays I could always watch the game. (habitual)

### Drills & artifacts

<!-- TODO: link existing pret/imp drills; add a poder-specific drill if one doesn't exist. -->

### Traps

- **"I could" is the trap.** English collapses both readings. Default-translating to *podia* often loses the "managed to" reading. If the sentence implies effort, completion, or a specific occasion, switch to *pude*.
- **Negative is especially tricky.** *Não pude* = didn't manage to (specific). *Não podia* = wasn't allowed to / wasn't able to (general). "I couldn't come yesterday" → *Não pude vir ontem*, not *não podia vir ontem*.
- *Pude* and *consegui* (preterite of *conseguir*) are near-synonyms in this aspect. Many native speakers use *consegui* even where *pude* would work.
- *Pôde* (third person, with the circumflex) is often misspelled or pronounced like *pode* (present); the accent is the only marker.

---

## Unit 51 — Querer: Aspectual Shift — quis vs queria

*Slug: `b1-querer-aspect-bp` · Sequence position: 46.9 · CEFR: B1 · Variant: bp*

**Concepts:** `aspectual-shift-querer`

**Prereqs:** `a2-pret-poder-querer-saber`, `a2-imp-regular`, `a2-pret-vs-imp`

### Outcomes

- Distinguish **quis** (acted on wanting / attempted / in negation, refused) from **queria** (wanted as an ongoing state, often unrealized)
- Recognize **não quis** as "refused," not "didn't want"
- Use **queria** for polite requests at counters, restaurants, on the phone (imperfeito de cortesia)

### Vocabulary

Triggering markers for **quis** (action taken on a desire):
- ontem, naquele momento, naquela hora
- mas / porém + a frustration: *quis falar, mas...*
- Negative: *não quis* = refused (a strong reading, not a soft "didn't want to")

Triggering markers for **queria** (ongoing desire, often unrealized):
- sempre, há anos, desde criança
- mas + a constraint: *queria viajar, mas não tive tempo*
- Polite request frame: *Eu queria um café, por favor.*

### Grammar

- **quis** = tried to / acted on wanting → punctual action driven by desire; in the negative, "refused"
- **queria** = wanted (state) → ongoing desire that may or may not have been acted on
- **queria** in present-time polite requests → softens the request below "quero" (which sounds blunt)

### Exemplar pairs

- *Eu **quis** falar com ele, mas estava ocupado.* — I tried to talk to him, but he was busy.
- *Eu **queria** falar com ele há semanas.* — I'd been wanting to talk to him for weeks.

- *Ele não **quis** vir.* — He refused to come. (active refusal)
- *Ele não **queria** vir.* — He didn't want to come. (state — may have come anyway)

- *Eu **quis** ajudar, mas ela recusou.* — I tried to help, but she refused.
- *Eu **queria** ajudar, mas não sabia como.* — I wanted to help, but didn't know how.

- *Eu **queria** um café, por favor.* — I'd like a coffee, please. (polite request)
- *Eu **quero** um café.* — I want a coffee. (direct, can sound blunt)

### Drills & artifacts

<!-- TODO: pair with the conditional / polite-request drills once authored. The polite-request reading of queria belongs here too. -->

### Traps

- **"He didn't want to" is not "ele não quis."** *Não quis* = "he refused" (active). For the neutral state-reading, use *não queria*. This is the highest-frequency error point.
- **"I wanted X" defaults to queria, not quis.** *Quis* implies an attempt; *queria* describes a desire. Default English "wanted" maps to *queria* in most contexts.
- **Polite-request queria is a register move, not an aspect move.** *Eu queria um café* is the standard counter-order register in BP; *eu quero um café* is grammatical but reads as terse or impatient. EP additionally uses *queria* heavily for politeness — covered in the EP twin.
- *Quis* in the affirmative often pairs with a frustration: *quis comprar, mas estava fechado* (tried to buy, but it was closed). If no frustration is in the air, the speaker probably means *queria*.

---

## Unit 52 — Pretérito perfeito composto (tenho falado) — uso habitual recente

*Slug: `b1-pret-perfeito-composto-bp` · Sequence position: 46.91 · CEFR: B1 · Variant: bp*

**Concepts:** `compound-tenses`

**Prereqs:** `a2-pret-regular-ar`, `a2-pret-regular-er-ir`

### Outcomes

After this unit, the student can:

- Form the pretérito perfeito composto (tenho/tens/tem/temos/têm + particípio passado) in BP
- Use it for **habitual or repeated action over a recent period**, almost always with a temporal adverb (*ultimamente, nesta semana, neste mês, nestes últimos dias*)
- Distinguish it from the pretérito perfeito simples (*comi* = ate once) — the compound is *not* the BP equivalent of English present perfect

### Vocabulary

- **tenho / tens / tem / temos / têm + particípio** — auxiliary + past participle
- Recency anchors that almost always accompany the form in BP:
  - *ultimamente* — lately
  - *nesta semana / neste mês / nestes últimos dias*
  - *recentemente*
  - *nos últimos tempos*

### Grammar

Form: presente do indicativo of *ter* + particípio passado.

| Pessoa | Auxiliar | + particípio |
|---|---|---|
| eu | tenho | falado |
| você / ele / ela | tem | falado |
| nós | temos | falado |
| vocês / eles / elas | têm | falado |

The BP reading is **iterative-recent**: the action has been happening repeatedly over a delimited recent period. It almost always pairs with an adverb that anchors the period. Without the adverb, the form sounds incomplete or EP-flavored to BP ears.

### Exemplar sentences

- *Tenho trabalhado muito ultimamente.* — I've been working a lot lately.
- *Ela tem estudado para a prova nesta semana.* — She's been studying for the exam this week.
- *Não tenho dormido bem nos últimos dias.* — I haven't been sleeping well lately.
- *Vocês têm visto a Maria?* — Have you been seeing Maria around?
- *Temos comido fora demais.* — We've been eating out too much.
- *Ele tem viajado muito a trabalho.* — He's been traveling a lot for work.

### Critical contrast with pretérito perfeito simples

| BP form | Reading | English |
|---|---|---|
| *Eu **comi** pizza ontem.* | one-time past event | I ate pizza yesterday. |
| *Eu **tenho comido** pizza ultimamente.* | recent-iterative | I've been eating pizza lately. |
| *Eu **tenho comido** pizza.* (no anchor) | sounds odd / EP-leaning in BP | (incomplete in BP register) |

### Drills & artifacts

<!-- TODO: link recency-adverb drills; pair with b1-pret-perfeito-composto-ep for variant-contrast practice. -->

### Traps

- **Don't translate English present perfect with this form.** *I have eaten / I have seen the movie* (one-time, single occurrence) → BP pretérito perfeito simples (*comi, vi*), NOT *tenho comido / tenho visto*. The compound carries iterative meaning in BP.
- **Always include the recency anchor in BP production.** *Tenho lido* alone sounds incomplete; *Tenho lido muito ultimamente* is natural.
- **EP usage is much broader.** EP students learn the same form for "I've been doing" without the obligatory adverb anchor — see `b1-pret-perfeito-composto-ep`. Recognize the EP usage when reading or listening; use the BP register in production.
- **Particípios irregulares matter here.** *Tenho dito* (irregular *dito* from *dizer*), *tenho feito* (*feito* from *fazer*), *tenho posto* (*posto* from *pôr*) — review irregular participles before drilling this unit.

---

## Unit 53 — Mais-que-perfeito do indicativo (tinha falado) — pluperfect

*Slug: `b1-mais-que-perfeito-ind` · Sequence position: 46.93 · CEFR: B1 · Variant: shared*

**Concepts:** `compound-tenses`, `preterite-imperfect`

**Prereqs:** `a2-pret-regular-ar`, `a2-pret-regular-er-ir`, `a2-imp-regular`, `a2-imp-irregular`

### Outcomes

After this unit, the student can:

- Form the mais-que-perfeito do indicativo (tinha/tinhas/tinha/tínhamos/tinham + particípio) — the **pluperfect**
- Use it to express a past action that occurred BEFORE another past action ("had done" in English)
- Sequence two past events correctly: simpler past + earlier past = pretérito perfeito + mais-que-perfeito

### Vocabulary

- **tinha / tinhas / tinha / tínhamos / tinham + particípio** — auxiliary + past participle
- Common signal words: *já* (already), *antes* (before), *quando* (when, sequencing), *depois que* (after)

### Grammar

Form: imperfeito do indicativo of *ter* + particípio passado.

| Pessoa | Auxiliar | + particípio |
|---|---|---|
| eu | tinha | falado |
| você / ele / ela | tinha | falado |
| nós | tínhamos | falado |
| vocês / eles / elas | tinham | falado |

The form anchors a past event **prior to** another past event. The reference point sits in the past, and the pluperfect points further back.

### Exemplar sentences

- *Quando cheguei, ele já **tinha saído**.* — When I arrived, he had already left.
- *Eu já **tinha visto** esse filme antes.* — I had already seen that movie before.
- *Eles **tinham terminado** o trabalho quando o chefe ligou.* — They had finished the work when the boss called.
- *Nunca **tínhamos comido** comida tão boa.* — We had never eaten such good food.
- *Vocês já **tinham conhecido** o Pedro antes da festa?* — Had you met Pedro before the party?
- *Ela me disse que **tinha estudado** muito.* — She told me she had studied a lot.

### Two-event sequencing

The pluperfect needs another past event as anchor. Without one, use pretérito perfeito simples instead:

- *Eu **vi** o filme.* — I saw the movie. (no anchor needed)
- *Eu já **tinha visto** o filme quando você me convidou.* — I had already seen the movie when you invited me. (anchored)

### Drills & artifacts

<!-- TODO: build a two-event sequencing drill — given two past events, identify which is the earlier one (pluperfect) and which is the anchor (preterite). -->

### Traps

- **Don't substitute pretérito perfeito for pluperfect when sequencing matters.** *Quando cheguei, ele saiu* loses the "before" relationship — implies he left at the moment you arrived. *Quando cheguei, ele já tinha saído* preserves the "had already left" reading.
- **Mais-que-perfeito simples (saíra, falara, vira) is literary.** In spoken BP and EP, the compound form (*tinha saído, tinha falado, tinha visto*) dominates. The simples form appears in formal writing, journalism, literary prose. Recognize it; don't produce it in conversation.
- **EP register substitution in conditionals.** EP often uses *tinha falado* as a substitute for *teria falado* (condicional composto) in counterfactual main clauses (*Se eu tivesse estudado, tinha passado*). BP keeps *teria passado*. This unit teaches the indicative pluperfect; the EP substitution pattern is covered in `b2-condicional-composto-bp` and its forthcoming EP twin.
- **Don't conflate with pretérito perfeito composto** (*tinha falado* vs *tenho falado*). The pluperfect anchors in the past; the *tenho* form anchors in the recent-up-to-now. Different temporal reference points.

---

## Unit 54 — Comparatives (mais...que, menos...que, tão...quanto)

*Slug: `a2-comparativos` · Sequence position: 47.0 · CEFR: A2 · Variant: shared*

**Concepts:** `adjective-comparison`

### Outcomes

- Compare two people or things using regular adjectives
- Make equality comparisons (as...as)
- Use irregular comparatives correctly (melhor, pior, maior, menor)
- Avoid common mistakes (mais bom, mais mau)
- Compare physical traits, qualities, cost, speed
- Combine comparatives with all tenses learned

### Vocabulary

- mais (more)
- menos (less)
- que / do que (than)
- tão...quanto (as...as)
- melhor (better - irregular)
- pior (worse - irregular)
- maior (bigger/older - irregular)
- menor (smaller/younger - irregular)

### Grammar

- **Structure 1: mais + adjective + que (more...than)**
- **Structure 2: menos + adjective + que (less...than)**
- **Structure 3: tão + adjective + quanto (as...as)**
- **Irregular comparatives:** melhor, pior, maior, menor (NEVER use mais bom, mais mau)

### Exemplar sentences

- João é mais alto que Pedro (João is taller than Pedro)
- Maria é menos rica que Ana (Maria is less rich than Ana)
- Sou tão velho quanto você (I'm as old as you)
- Este livro é melhor que aquele (This book is better than that one)
- São Paulo é maior que o Rio (São Paulo is bigger than Rio)
- Este restaurante é mais caro que aquele (This restaurant is more expensive than that one)

### Drills & artifacts

<!-- TODO: link drills, worksheets, lessons in Phase 3 -->

### Traps

<!-- TODO: enrich in Phase 3 -->

---

## Unit 55 — Superlatives (O mais..., O menos...)

*Slug: `a2-superlativos` · Sequence position: 48.0 · CEFR: A2 · Variant: shared*

**Concepts:** `adjective-comparison`

### Outcomes

- Express superlatives (the most/least)
- Use correct article agreement
- Use irregular superlatives correctly
- Define scope with "de" (of/in)
- Make absolute comparisons within a group
- Distinguish comparative (Unit 47) from superlative

### Vocabulary

- **o mais** (the most)
- **o menos** (the least)
- **de** (of/in - for scope)
- **do mundo** (in the world)
- **do Brasil** (in Brazil)
- **da cidade** (in the city)
- **da família** (in the family)
- **da classe** (in the class)

### Grammar

- **Superlative structure:** article + mais/menos + adjective + de + scope
  - **o mais** alto **da** classe (the tallest in the class)
  - **a mais** bonita **do** Brasil (the most beautiful in Brazil)
- **Article agrees with the noun:**
  - o mais... (masculine singular)
  - a mais... (feminine singular)
  - os mais... (masculine plural)
  - as mais... (feminine plural)
- **Irregular superlatives:**
  - o **melhor** (the best) - NOT "o mais bom"
  - o **pior** (the worst) - NOT "o mais mau"
  - o **maior** (the biggest/oldest) - NOT "o mais grande" (in most cases)
  - o **menor** (the smallest/youngest) - NOT "o mais pequeno"

### Exemplar sentences

- Ele é o mais alto da turma (He's the tallest in the class)
- Esta é a mais bonita cidade do Brasil (This is the most beautiful city in Brazil)
- São Paulo é a maior cidade do país (São Paulo is the biggest city in the country)
- Este é o melhor restaurante da cidade (This is the best restaurant in the city)
- Ela é a mais nova da família (She's the youngest in the family)
- Este foi o pior dia da minha vida (This was the worst day of my life)
- Ele é o menos simpático do grupo (He's the least friendly in the group)

### Drills & artifacts

<!-- TODO: link drills, worksheets, lessons in Phase 3 -->

### Traps

<!-- TODO: enrich in Phase 3 -->

## Unit 56 — Telling Time (Que horas são?)

*Slug: `a1-horas` · Sequence position: 49.0 · CEFR: A1 · Variant: shared*

**Concepts:** `time-expressions`

### Outcomes

- Ask what time it is
- Tell time on the hour
- Tell time with minutes (past and to the hour)
- Use special expressions (meio-dia, meia-noite)
- Distinguish AM from PM (da manhã/da tarde/da noite)
- Schedule appointments and meetings

### Vocabulary

- **hora/horas** (hour/hours, o'clock)
- **meio-dia** (noon - literally "half-day")
- **meia-noite** (midnight - literally "half-night")
- **meio/meia** (half)
- **quinze** (quarter - 15 minutes)
- **menos** (minus, to - for "to the hour")
- **para** (to - alternate for "to the hour")
- **em ponto** (on the dot, exactly)
- **da manhã** (in the morning - AM)
- **da tarde** (in the afternoon - PM)
- **da noite** (at night - PM)
- **madrugada** (early morning hours - 1-5 AM)

### Grammar

- **Question:** Que horas são? (What time is it? - literally "What hours are they?")
  - Note: PLURAL "são" because time is plural concept
- **Exception:** É uma hora (It's 1 o'clock - SINGULAR for 1:00 only!)
- **Structure patterns:**
  - **On the hour:** São [number] horas
  - **Past the hour:** São [hour] e [minutes]
  - **Half past:** São [hour] e meia (literally "and half")
  - **Quarter past:** São [hour] e quinze
  - **To the hour:** São [minutes] para as [next hour] OR Faltam [minutes] para as [next hour]
- **12-hour system** (Brazil uses 12-hour more commonly than 24-hour in speech)

### Drills & artifacts

## Unit 57 — Days of the Week (Dias da Semana)

*Slug: `a1-dias-semana` · Sequence position: 50.0 · CEFR: A1 · Variant: shared*

**Concepts:** `days-of-week`

### Outcomes

- Name all seven days of the week
- Ask and answer what day it is
- Say when events happen (on Monday, on Saturday)
- Use shortened forms (segunda vs segunda-feira)
- Express recurring events (every Monday, on Saturdays)
- Talk about the weekend

### Vocabulary

- **semana** (week)
- **dia/dias** (day/days)
- **Days of the week:**
  - segunda-feira (Monday - literally "second fair/market day")
  - terça-feira (Tuesday - literally "third fair day")
  - quarta-feira (Wednesday - literally "fourth fair day")
  - quinta-feira (Thursday - literally "fifth fair day")
  - sexta-feira (Friday - literally "sixth fair day")
  - sábado (Saturday)
  - domingo (Sunday)
- **fim de semana** (weekend)
- **dia útil** (weekday - literally "useful day")
- **hoje** (today)
- **amanhã** (tomorrow)
- **ontem** (yesterday)

### Grammar

- **Days are MASCULINE** (o domingo, o sábado)
- **Days with "feira"** can drop "-feira" in speech: segunda, terça, quarta, quinta, sexta
- **Preposition "em" for "on"** a specific day:
  - na segunda(-feira) (on Monday)
  - no sábado (on Saturday)
  - no domingo (on Sunday)
- **Plural for recurring days:**
  - às segundas (on Mondays - every Monday)
  - aos sábados (on Saturdays - every Saturday)
- **NO article** for "today": hoje é segunda (today is Monday) - NOT "hoje é a segunda"

### Exemplar sentences

- Hoje é sexta-feira (Today is Friday)
- Amanhã é sábado (Tomorrow is Saturday)
- Ontem foi quinta-feira (Yesterday was Thursday)
- Trabalho de segunda a sexta (I work Monday to Friday)
- Vou viajar no domingo (I'm going to travel on Sunday)
- Tenho aula na terça (I have class on Tuesday)
- Aos sábados eu acordo tarde (On Saturdays I wake up late)
- Que dia é hoje? (What day is today?)
- O fim de semana começa na sexta (The weekend starts on Friday)

## Unit 58 — Months of the Year (Meses do Ano)

*Slug: `a1-meses` · Sequence position: 51.0 · CEFR: A1 · Variant: shared*

**Concepts:** `months`

### Outcomes

- Name all twelve months
- Say when birthdays occur (in which month)
- Say when events happen (in January, in July)
- Ask what month it is
- Express birth month
- Talk about past, present, and future months

### Vocabulary

- **mês/meses** (month/months)
- **ano** (year)
- **Months:**
  - janeiro (January)
  - fevereiro (February)
  - março (March)
  - abril (April)
  - maio (May)
  - junho (June)
  - julho (July)
  - agosto (August)
  - setembro (September)
  - outubro (October)
  - novembro (November)
  - dezembro (December)
- **próximo/próxima** (next)
- **passado/passada** (last)
- **este/esta** (this)

### Grammar

- **Months are MASCULINE** (o janeiro, o maio)
- **Preposition "em" for "in"** a month:
  - em janeiro (in January)
  - em março (in March)
- **NO article** needed: "em janeiro" NOT "no janeiro"
- **Capitalization:** Months are NOT capitalized in Portuguese (unlike English)
- **Dates use "de":** "5 de maio" (May 5th - literally "5 of May")

### Exemplar sentences

- Meu aniversário é em maio (My birthday is in May)
- Estamos em novembro (We are in November / It is November)
- Vou viajar em julho (I'm going to travel in July)
- Nasci em março de 1995 (I was born in March 1995)
- O verão começa em dezembro no Brasil (Summer starts in December in Brazil)
- Em que mês estamos? (What month is it?)
- Faço aniversário em setembro (I have my birthday in September)
- O ano começa em janeiro (The year starts in January)

## Unit 59 — Dates (Calendar Dates - Dia, Mês, Ano)

*Slug: `a1-datas` · Sequence position: 52.0 · CEFR: A1 · Variant: shared*

**Concepts:** `dates`

### Outcomes

- Give today's complete date
- State their birth date
- Schedule events with full dates
- Read and write dates in Portuguese format (dd/mm/yyyy)
- Use "primeiro" for the 1st of any month
- Express dates in past, present, and future

### Vocabulary

- **data** (date)
- **dia** (day - the number)
- **primeiro** (first - 1st of month)
- **hoje** (today)
- **amanhã** (tomorrow)
- **ontem** (yesterday)
- **Que dia é hoje?** (What's today's date?)
- **quando** (when)
- **nascimento** (birth)
- **data de nascimento** (date of birth)

### Grammar

- **Date format:** day + de + month + de + year
  - 5 de maio de 2024 (May 5, 2024)
- **First of month:** Use "primeiro" NOT "um"
  - 1 de janeiro (January 1st - literally "first of January")
  - primeiro de janeiro (January 1st)
- **All other days:** Use cardinal numbers (dois, três, quatro...)
  - 2 de janeiro (January 2nd)
  - 15 de março (March 15th)
- **Question:** Que dia é hoje? (What's today's date?)
- **Answer:** Hoje é [day] de [month] (Today is [month] [day])
- **Written format:** dd/mm/yyyy (day/month/year - opposite of US!)
  - 05/05/2024 = May 5, 2024
  - 25/12/2024 = December 25, 2024

### Exemplar sentences

- Hoje é 25 de novembro de 2024 (Today is November 25, 2024)
- Meu aniversário é em 10 de julho (My birthday is on July 10th)
- Nasci no dia 5 de março de 1990 (I was born on March 5, 1990)
- A reunião é no dia primeiro de dezembro (The meeting is on December 1st)
- Vou viajar no dia 20 de junho (I'm going to travel on June 20th)
- Que dia é hoje? (What's today's date?)
- O Natal é no dia 25 de dezembro (Christmas is on December 25th)
- O Ano Novo é primeiro de janeiro (New Year's is January 1st)

## Unit 60 — Ordinal Numbers (Primeiro, Segundo, Terceiro...)

*Slug: `a1-num-ordinais` · Sequence position: 53.0 · CEFR: A1 · Variant: shared*

**Concepts:** `numbers`

### Outcomes

- Use ordinal numbers for floors (1st-10th)
- Use "primeiro" for 1st of any month (from Unit 52)
- Express positions and rankings
- Describe sequences (first time, second attempt, etc.)
- Understand ordinal abbreviations (1º, 2ª, 3º)
- Apply correct gender agreement

### Vocabulary

- **Ordinal numbers 1st-10th:**
  - primeiro/primeira (first - 1st)
  - segundo/segunda (second - 2nd)
  - terceiro/terceira (third - 3rd)
  - quarto/quarta (fourth - 4th)
  - quinto/quinta (fifth - 5th)
  - sexto/sexta (sixth - 6th)
  - sétimo/sétima (seventh - 7th)
  - oitavo/oitava (eighth - 8th)
  - nono/nona (ninth - 9th)
  - décimo/décima (tenth - 10th)
- **andar** (floor - in building)
- **lugar** (place, position)
- **posição** (position)
- **classificação** (ranking, classification)

### Grammar

- **Ordinal numbers have gender agreement:** primeiro/primeira, segundo/segunda
- **Used for:**
  - Floors: "primeiro andar" (first floor), "terceiro andar" (third floor)
  - Dates: "primeiro de maio" (May 1st) - ONLY for 1st of month!
  - Positions: "primeiro lugar" (first place)
  - Sequences: "a primeira vez" (the first time)
  - Royalty: "Dom Pedro Segundo" (Dom Pedro the Second)
- **Position:** ordinal + noun (like other adjectives)
- **Abbreviations:** 1º (masc), 1ª (fem), 2º, 3º, etc.
- **After 10th:** Usually use cardinal numbers instead
  - o décimo primeiro andar (11th floor - formal)
  - o andar onze (floor 11 - more common)

### Exemplar sentences

- Moro no segundo andar (I live on the second floor)
- O escritório fica no quinto andar (The office is on the fifth floor)
- Esta é minha primeira vez aqui (This is my first time here)
- Ele é o terceiro da fila (He's third in line)
- A segunda porta à esquerda (The second door on the left)
- O primeiro dia de aula (The first day of class)
- Fiquei em quarto lugar (I came in fourth place)
- Vou pela terceira vez (I'm going for the third time)

## Unit 61 — Weather Expressions (Tempo e Clima)

*Slug: `a2-tempo-clima` · Sequence position: 54.0 · CEFR: A2 · Variant: shared*

**Concepts:** `weather`

### Outcomes

- Ask about the weather
- Describe current weather conditions
- Use FAZER vs ESTAR correctly for weather
- Talk about temperature
- Describe seasons and their typical weather
- Express weather in different tenses

### Vocabulary

- **tempo** (weather)
- **clima** (climate)
- **Weather expressions with FAZER:**
  - faz calor (it's hot)
  - faz frio (it's cold)
  - faz sol (it's sunny)
  - faz vento (it's windy)
- **Weather with ESTAR:**
  - está quente (it's hot/warm)
  - está frio (it's cold)
  - está nublado (it's cloudy)
  - está ensolarado (it's sunny)
- **Weather verbs:**
  - chove / está chovendo (it's raining)
  - neva / está nevando (it's snowing - rare in Brazil!)
- **Temperature:**
  - graus (degrees)
  - calor (heat)
  - frio (cold)
  - quente (hot)
- **Adjectives:**
  - úmido (humid)
  - seco (dry)
  - agradável (pleasant)

### Grammar

- **FAZER for general weather:** Faz calor (It's hot)
  - Impersonal use of fazer (3rd person singular only)
  - No subject needed
- **ESTAR for current conditions:** Está quente (It's warm)
  - Describes current state
- **Weather verbs (impersonal):** Chove (It rains) / Está chovendo (It's raining)
- **Preposition "em":** "No Brasil faz calor" (In Brazil it's hot)
- **Degrees:** "Está 30 graus" (It's 30 degrees)

### Exemplar sentences

- Faz calor hoje (It's hot today)
- Está chovendo (It's raining)
- Como está o tempo? (How's the weather?)
- Faz muito frio no inverno (It's very cold in winter)
- Está quente e úmido (It's hot and humid)
- Que tempo faz aí? (What's the weather like there?)
- Está 35 graus (It's 35 degrees)
- Faz sol o ano todo (It's sunny all year round)
- No Rio sempre faz calor (In Rio it's always hot)

## Unit 62 — Colors (Cores Básicas)

*Slug: `a1-cores` · Sequence position: 55.0 · CEFR: A1 · Variant: shared*

**Concepts:** `colors`

### Outcomes

- Name 11 basic colors
- Describe objects by color with correct agreement
- Ask what color something is
- Combine colors with previously learned nouns (casa, carro, livro, etc.)
- Make simple statements about color preferences

### Vocabulary

- **Basic colors:**
  - branco/branca (white)
  - preto/preta (black)
  - vermelho/vermelha (red)
  - azul (blue)
  - verde (green)
  - amarelo/amarela (yellow)
  - laranja (orange - invariable)
  - rosa (pink - invariable)
  - marrom (brown - invariable)
  - cinza (gray - invariable)
  - roxo/roxa (purple)

### Grammar

- **Color adjectives agree in gender and number with the noun:**
  - o carro **vermelho** (the red car - masculine)
  - a casa **vermelha** (the red house - feminine)
  - os carros **vermelhos** (the red cars - masculine plural)
  - as casas **vermelhas** (the red houses - feminine plural)

- **EXCEPTION: Invariable colors (no gender/number change):**
  - **laranja** (orange): uma casa laranja, um carro laranja
  - **rosa** (pink): uma casa rosa, um carro rosa
  - **marrom** (brown): uma casa marrom, um carro marrom
  - **cinza** (gray): uma casa cinza, um carro cinza

- **Color placement:** Colors come AFTER the noun in Portuguese
  - ✅ carro azul (blue car)
  - ❌ azul carro (wrong word order)

- **Asking about color:** De que cor é? (What color is it?)
  - De que cor é o carro? (What color is the car?)
  - É azul. (It's blue.)

### Exemplar sentences

- A casa é branca. (The house is white.)
- O carro é azul. (The car is blue.)
- De que cor é a camisa? (What color is the shirt?)
- Meu livro é verde. (My book is green.)
- A porta é marrom. (The door is brown.)
- Eu gosto de vermelho. (I like red.)
- As flores são rosas. (The flowers are pink.)

## Unit 63 — Clothing Basics (Roupas Básicas)

*Slug: `a1-roupas` · Sequence position: 56.0 · CEFR: A1 · Variant: shared*

**Concepts:** `clothing`

### Outcomes

- Name 11 essential clothing items
- Use correct gender for clothing vocabulary
- Describe what they're wearing with USAR
- Combine clothing with colors from Unit 55
- Ask what others are wearing

### Vocabulary

- **Essential clothing items:**
  - a camisa (shirt - feminine!)
  - a camiseta (t-shirt - feminine)
  - a calça (pants - singular in Portuguese!)
  - a saia (skirt)
  - o vestido (dress)
  - o casaco (jacket/coat)
  - o sapato (shoe)
  - a meia (sock)
  - o chapéu (hat)
  - os óculos (glasses - always plural)
  - a roupa (clothing - singular means "clothes")

### Grammar

- **Gender surprises in clothing:**
  - **camisa is FEMININE** even though it often refers to men's shirts
  - **vestido is MASCULINE** even though dresses are typically worn by women
  - Gender is about the word, not who wears it!

- **Singular/Plural differences from English:**
  - **calça** (pants) is SINGULAR in Portuguese:
    - ✅ "Eu uso **uma** calça" (I'm wearing pants)
    - ❌ "Eu uso calças" (sounds like multiple pairs)
  - **óculos** (glasses) is PLURAL in both languages:
    - "Eu uso óculos" (I wear glasses)

- **Wearing/Using:** USAR (to wear/use)
  - Eu uso uma camisa. (I'm wearing a shirt.)
  - Você usa óculos? (Do you wear glasses?)
  - Ela usa vestido. (She's wearing a dress.)

- **Verbs for getting dressed:**
  - **vestir** (to dress/wear): Eu visto uma camisa. (I put on/wear a shirt.)
  - **usar** (to use/wear): Eu uso sapatos. (I wear shoes.)
  - More common: usar (simpler, more versatile)

### Exemplar sentences

- Eu uso uma camisa branca. (I'm wearing a white shirt.)
- Ela usa um vestido vermelho. (She's wearing a red dress.)
- Você usa óculos? (Do you wear glasses?)
- Meu sapato é preto. (My shoe is black.)
- Ele usa uma calça azul. (He's wearing blue pants.)
- Eu preciso de um casaco. (I need a jacket.)
- A saia é verde. (The skirt is green.)

### Drills & artifacts

<!-- TODO: link drills, worksheets, lessons in Phase 3 -->

### Traps

<!-- TODO: enrich in Phase 3 -->

## Unit 64 — Body Parts (Partes do Corpo)

*Slug: `a1-corpo` · Sequence position: 57.0 · CEFR: A1 · Variant: shared*

**Concepts:** `body-parts`

### Outcomes

- Name 14 essential body parts
- Use correct irregular plurals (mãos, pés)
- Describe pain or problems with body parts
- Use the verb DOER correctly with body parts
- Describe physical features (hair color, eye color)

### Vocabulary

- **Basic body parts:**
  - a cabeça (head)
  - o cabelo (hair)
  - o olho (eye)
  - a orelha (ear)
  - o nariz (nose)
  - a boca (mouth)
  - o dente (tooth)
  - o braço (arm)
  - a mão (hand)
  - o dedo (finger/toe)
  - a perna (leg)
  - o pé (foot)
  - a barriga (belly/stomach)
  - as costas (back - always plural)

### Grammar

- **Plural forms with body parts:**
  - **os olhos** (eyes - plural)
  - **as mãos** (hands - irregular plural! not "maos")
  - **os pés** (feet - irregular plural! not "pes")
  - **as costas** (back - ALWAYS plural in Portuguese)

- **Describing pain/problems with body parts:**
  - Use DOER (to hurt) - special verb:
    - "**Meu** braço **dói**" (My arm hurts)
    - "**Minha** cabeça **dói**" (My head hurts)
    - "**Meus** olhos **doem**" (My eyes hurt - plural verb!)
  - Structure: possessive + body part + doer (conjugated)

- **The verb DOER (to hurt):**
  - 3rd person ONLY (body part is the subject doing the hurting)
  - **Singular:** dói (one thing hurts)
  - **Plural:** doem (multiple things hurt)
  - Examples:
    - O pé dói. (The foot hurts.)
    - Os pés doem. (The feet hurt.)

### Exemplar sentences

- Minha cabeça dói. (My head hurts.)
- Meus olhos são azuis. (My eyes are blue.)
- Meu cabelo é preto. (My hair is black.)
- Meus pés doem. (My feet hurt.)
- Eu tenho dor de barriga. (I have a stomachache.)
- Minhas mãos são pequenas. (My hands are small.)
- O braço dele dói. (His arm hurts.)

### Drills & artifacts

<!-- TODO: link drills, worksheets, lessons in Phase 3 -->

### Traps

<!-- TODO: enrich in Phase 3 -->

## Unit 65 — Family Members Expanded (Família - Detalhada)

*Slug: `a1-familia` · Sequence position: 58.0 · CEFR: A1 · Variant: shared*

**Concepts:** `family`

### Outcomes

- Name 17 family members (beyond immediate family)
- Describe extended family relationships
- Use collective masculine plurals (avós, primos, etc.)
- Ask and answer questions about family
- Combine with numbers from Units 44-45

### Vocabulary

<!-- TODO: enrich in Phase 3 -->

### Grammar

- **Collective masculine plural:**
  - **os avós** (grandparents - both genders)
  - **os netos** (grandchildren - both genders)
  - **os primos** (cousins - both genders)
  - **os tios** (aunt and uncle together)
  - When mixed gender, use masculine plural

- **Possessives with family (review + expansion):**
  - meu avô (my grandfather)
  - minha avó (my grandmother)
  - meus avós (my grandparents)
  - minhas primas (my female cousins)

- **Asking about family:**
  - Você tem irmãos? (Do you have siblings? - literally "brothers")
  - Você tem primos? (Do you have cousins?)
  - Quantos primos você tem? (How many cousins do you have?)
  - Como é sua família? (What's your family like?)

### Exemplar sentences

- Eu tenho dois avós. (I have two grandparents.)
- Minha avó tem 75 anos. (My grandmother is 75 years old.)
- Meu tio mora no Brasil. (My uncle lives in Brazil.)
- Eu tenho três primos. (I have three cousins.)
- Meus netos são pequenos. (My grandchildren are small.)
- Minha tia é professora. (My aunt is a teacher.)
- Eu visito meus avós no domingo. (I visit my grandparents on Sunday.)

## Unit 66 — Emotions and Feelings (Emoções e Sentimentos)

*Slug: `a2-emocoes` · Sequence position: 59.0 · CEFR: A2 · Variant: shared*

**Concepts:** `emotions`, `expressing-opinions`

### Outcomes

- Name 12 common emotions and feelings
- Use ESTAR correctly with emotion adjectives
- Use TER correctly with fome/sede/sono/medo
- Ask how someone is feeling
- Describe why they feel a certain way
- Distinguish temporary feelings (estar) from personality (ser)

### Vocabulary

- **Basic emotions:**
  - feliz (happy)
  - triste (sad)
  - cansado/cansada (tired)
  - animado/animada (excited/energetic)
  - nervoso/nervosa (nervous)
  - com raiva (angry - literally "with anger")
  - preocupado/preocupada (worried)
  - assustado/assustada (scared/frightened)
  - entediado/entediada (bored)
  - com fome (hungry - literally "with hunger")
  - com sede (thirsty - literally "with thirst")
  - com sono (sleepy - literally "with sleep")

### Grammar

- **Emotions with ESTAR (not SER):**
  - Emotions are TEMPORARY states → use ESTAR
  - ✅ "Eu **estou** feliz" (I am happy - right now)
  - ❌ "Eu **sou** feliz" (wrong for current feeling - would mean personality trait)

- **Emotions using TER (to have):**
  - Some emotions/physical feelings use TER + "com" construction:
    - "Eu **tenho** fome" (I'm hungry - literally "I have hunger")
    - "Eu **tenho** sede" (I'm thirsty - literally "I have thirst")
    - "Eu **tenho** sono" (I'm sleepy - literally "I have sleep")
    - "Eu **tenho** medo" (I'm afraid - literally "I have fear")
  - Alternative: Eu estou **com** fome/sede/sono (I am with hunger/thirst/sleep)

- **Asking about feelings:**
  - "Como você está?" (How are you? - asking about current state)
  - "Como você se sente?" (How do you feel?)
  - "Você está bem?" (Are you okay?)
  - "O que você tem?" (What's wrong? - literally "What do you have?")

### Exemplar sentences

- Eu estou feliz. (I'm happy.)
- Ela está triste. (She's sad.)
- Estou muito cansado. (I'm very tired.)
- Você está nervoso? (Are you nervous?)
- Eu tenho fome. (I'm hungry.)
- Estamos animados! (We're excited!)
- Ele está preocupado. (He's worried.)

## Unit 67 — Locations and Directions (Localizações e Direções)

*Slug: `a2-localizacoes-direcoes` · Sequence position: 60.0 · CEFR: A2 · Variant: shared*

**Concepts:** `directions`

### Outcomes

- Describe where objects are located
- Use 13 prepositions of place correctly
- Contract "de" and "em" with articles (do, da, no, na)
- Give and understand basic directions
- Ask and answer "Onde está?" (Where is?)

### Vocabulary

- **Prepositions of place:**
  - em (in/on/at)
  - dentro de (inside of)
  - fora de (outside of)
  - em cima de (on top of)
  - embaixo de (under/below)
  - ao lado de (next to/beside)
  - perto de (near/close to)
  - longe de (far from)
  - na frente de (in front of)
  - atrás de (behind)
  - entre (between)
  - acima de (above)
  - abaixo de (below)

- **Direction words:**
  - à direita (to the right)
  - à esquerda (to the left)
  - em frente (straight ahead)
  - para cima (upward)
  - para baixo (downward)

### Grammar

- **Compound prepositions require "de":**
  - ✅ em cima **de** (on top of) - requires "de"
  - ✅ ao lado **de** (next to) - requires "de"
  - ✅ perto **de** (near) - requires "de"
  - Must be followed by "de" before the noun

- **Contraction of "de" with articles:**
  - de + o = **do** (of the - masculine)
  - de + a = **da** (of the - feminine)
  - de + os = **dos** (of the - masculine plural)
  - de + as = **das** (of the - feminine plural)

  Examples:
  - em cima **do** carro (on top of the car)
  - perto **da** casa (near the house)
  - ao lado **dos** livros (next to the books)

- **EM contracts with articles:**
  - em + o = **no** (in/on/at the - masculine)
  - em + a = **na** (in/on/at the - feminine)
  - em + os = **nos** (in/on/at the - masculine plural)
  - em + as = **nas** (in/on/at the - feminine plural)

### Exemplar sentences

- O livro está em cima da mesa. (The book is on top of the table.)
- A casa fica perto do parque. (The house is near the park.)
- O gato está embaixo da cama. (The cat is under the bed.)
- O banco fica ao lado da farmácia. (The bank is next to the pharmacy.)
- Onde está o banheiro? - À direita. (Where's the bathroom? - To the right.)
- A escola fica longe da minha casa. (The school is far from my house.)
- O carro está na frente da casa. (The car is in front of the house.)

## Unit 68 — House and Rooms (Casa e Cômodos)

*Slug: `a1-casa-comodos` · Sequence position: 61.0 · CEFR: A1 · Variant: shared*

**Concepts:** `house-rooms`

### Outcomes

- Name 17 parts of a house/apartment
- Describe how many rooms their house has
- Say where they are in the house: "Estou no quarto"
- Use MORAR to say where they live
- Combine with numbers from Units 44-45

### Vocabulary

- **Parts of a house:**
  - a casa (house)
  - o apartamento (apartment)
  - o quarto (bedroom)
  - a sala (living room)
  - a sala de estar (living room - formal)
  - a sala de jantar (dining room)
  - a cozinha (kitchen)
  - o banheiro (bathroom)
  - o quarto de banho (bathroom - European Portuguese)
  - a garagem (garage)
  - o jardim (garden/yard)
  - a varanda (balcony/porch)
  - o corredor (hallway)
  - a escada (staircase)
  - o telhado (roof)
  - a porta (door)
  - a janela (window)

### Grammar

- **Using rooms with prepositions:**
  - **no** quarto (in the bedroom - masculine)
  - **na** cozinha (in the kitchen - feminine)
  - **na** sala (in the living room - feminine)
  - Remember: em + o = no, em + a = na

- **Expressing possession of rooms:**
  - Minha casa tem três quartos. (My house has three bedrooms.)
  - Meu apartamento tem dois banheiros. (My apartment has two bathrooms.)
  - Use TER (to have) to describe what's in the house

- **MORAR vs VIVER (to live):**
  - Both mean "to live" but slightly different usage:
  - **MORAR** = to reside, live in (more common for address)
    - "Eu moro em uma casa" (I live in a house)
    - "Eu moro no apartamento" (I live in the apartment)
  - **VIVER** = to live, exist (more general/philosophical)
    - "Eu vivo no Brasil" (I live in Brazil)

### Exemplar sentences

- Eu moro em uma casa. (I live in a house.)
- Minha casa tem três quartos. (My house has three bedrooms.)
- Eu estou na cozinha. (I'm in the kitchen.)
- O banheiro fica ao lado do quarto. (The bathroom is next to the bedroom.)
- Meu apartamento tem uma varanda. (My apartment has a balcony.)
- A sala é grande. (The living room is big.)
- Onde está o banheiro? - No corredor, à direita. (Where's the bathroom? - In the hallway, on the right.)

## Unit 69 — Daily Activities Verbs (Verbos de Atividades Diárias)

*Slug: `a2-atividades-diarias` · Sequence position: 62.0 · CEFR: A2 · Variant: shared*

**Concepts:** `common-expressions`

### Outcomes

- Name 17 daily activity verbs
- Conjugate regular daily routine verbs in present tense
- Use irregular DORMIR correctly
- Describe their daily routine with times
- Sequence activities in order

### Vocabulary

- **Daily routine verbs:**
  - acordar (to wake up)
  - levantar (to get up)
  - tomar banho (to take a shower/bath)
  - escovar (to brush)
  - pentear (to comb)
  - vestir (to dress/get dressed)
  - tomar café (to have breakfast - literally "take coffee")
  - almoçar (to have lunch)
  - jantar (to have dinner)
  - estudar (to study)
  - trabalhar (to work) [review]
  - descansar (to rest)
  - assistir (to watch)
  - dormir (to sleep)
  - cozinhar (to cook)
  - limpar (to clean)
  - lavar (to wash)

### Grammar

- **All verbs are regular except DORMIR:**
  - **DORMIR (to sleep)** is irregular (o → ue stem change in some forms):
    - eu durmo (I sleep)
    - você dorme (you sleep)
    - ele/ela dorme (he/she sleeps)
    - nós dormimos (we sleep)
    - vocês dormem (you all sleep)
    - eles/elas dormem (they sleep)

- **Reflexive use with daily routine:**
  - Some activities can be reflexive (doing to yourself):
  - **vestir-se** (to get dressed - literally "dress oneself")
  - **pentear-se** (to comb one's hair)
  - **levantar-se** (to get up - literally "lift oneself")
  - More common in formal speech; often dropped in casual Brazilian Portuguese

- **Time expressions with daily activities:**
  - Eu acordo **às** sete horas. (I wake up at 7 o'clock.)
  - Eu almoço **ao meio-dia**. (I have lunch at noon.)
  - Eu durmo **à** noite. (I sleep at night.)
  - Use **às** (at) with specific times

### Exemplar sentences

- Eu acordo às sete da manhã. (I wake up at 7 AM.)
- Eu tomo banho todos os dias. (I shower every day.)
- Ela escova os dentes. (She brushes her teeth.)
- Nós almoçamos ao meio-dia. (We have lunch at noon.)
- Eu trabalho de segunda a sexta. (I work Monday to Friday.)
- Ele dorme oito horas por noite. (He sleeps eight hours per night.)
- Eu cozinho o jantar. (I cook dinner.)

## Unit 70 — Frequency Adverbs (Advérbios de Frequência)

*Slug: `a2-adv-frequencia` · Sequence position: 63.0 · CEFR: A2 · Variant: shared*

**Concepts:** `adverbs-frequency`

### Outcomes

- Use 9 frequency adverbs correctly
- Express how often they do activities
- Use "todo/toda" with correct gender agreement
- Count frequency (once, twice, three times per...)
- Describe habits and routines precisely

### Vocabulary

- **Frequency adverbs:**
  - sempre (always)
  - quase sempre (almost always)
  - geralmente (generally/usually)
  - normalmente (normally)
  - às vezes (sometimes)
  - de vez em quando (once in a while)
  - raramente (rarely)
  - quase nunca (almost never)
  - nunca (never)

- **Time frequency expressions:**
  - todo dia (every day)
  - todos os dias (every day - plural)
  - toda semana (every week)
  - todo mês (every month)
  - todo ano (every year)
  - uma vez por semana (once a week)
  - duas vezes por dia (twice a day)
  - três vezes por mês (three times a month)

### Grammar

- **Adverb placement (flexible but patterns exist):**

  **Option 1 - Before the verb (most common):**
  - Eu **sempre** acordo às sete. (I always wake up at 7.)
  - Ela **nunca** come carne. (She never eats meat.)
  - Nós **geralmente** almoçamos em casa. (We usually have lunch at home.)

  **Option 2 - After the verb (emphasis or style):**
  - Eu acordo **sempre** às sete. (I wake up always at 7 - emphasis)
  - Less common, more emphatic

  **Option 3 - Beginning of sentence (emphasis):**
  - **Sempre** eu acordo às sete. (Always I wake up at 7 - rare, emphatic)

- **NUNCA with negation:**
  - Portuguese allows double negatives!
  - Eu **nunca** como carne. (I never eat meat.) - most common
  - Eu **não** como carne **nunca**. (I don't eat meat never.) - also correct!
  - Both are grammatically correct in Portuguese

- **TODO/TODA agreement:**
  - **todo** (every - masculine singular): todo dia (every day)
  - **toda** (every - feminine singular): toda semana (every week)
  - **todos** (every/all - masculine plural): todos os dias (every day)
  - **todas** (every/all - feminine plural): todas as semanas (every week)

### Exemplar sentences

- Eu sempre tomo café da manhã. (I always have breakfast.)
- Ela nunca chega atrasada. (She never arrives late.)
- Nós geralmente almoçamos juntos. (We usually have lunch together.)
- Eu vou ao cinema duas vezes por mês. (I go to the movies twice a month.)
- Ele raramente cozinha. (He rarely cooks.)
- Eu estudo todos os dias. (I study every day.)
- De vez em quando eu durmo tarde. (Once in a while I sleep late.)

## Unit 71 — Food and Meals Expanded (Comida e Refeições)

*Slug: `a2-comida-refeicoes` · Sequence position: 64.0 · CEFR: A2 · Variant: shared*

**Concepts:** `food-meals`

### Outcomes

- Name 28 common foods and drinks
- Use correct gender for food vocabulary
- Express food preferences with gostar de
- Order food and describe meals
- Use basic quantity expressions

### Vocabulary

- **Proteins:**
  - a carne (meat)
  - o frango (chicken)
  - o peixe (fish)
  - o ovo (egg)
  - o queijo (cheese)

- **Vegetables:**
  - a alface (lettuce)
  - o tomate (tomato)
  - a cenoura (carrot)
  - a batata (potato)
  - a cebola (onion)

- **Fruits:**
  - a maçã (apple)
  - a banana (banana)
  - a laranja (orange)
  - o morango (strawberry)
  - a uva (grape)

- **Staples:**
  - o arroz (rice)
  - o feijão (beans)
  - o pão (bread)
  - a massa (pasta)
  - o açúcar (sugar)
  - o sal (salt)

- **Drinks:**
  - a água (water)
  - o suco (juice)
  - o refrigerante (soda)
  - o leite (milk)

### Grammar

- **Using food with verbs:**
  - **comer** (to eat) + food: "Eu como arroz" (I eat rice)
  - **beber** (to drink) + beverage: "Eu bebo água" (I drink water)
  - **gostar de** (to like) + food: "Eu gosto de frango" (I like chicken)

- **Gender surprises in food vocabulary:**
  - **o tomate** (tomato - masculine, even though ends in -e)
  - **o leite** (milk - masculine)
  - **a carne** (meat - feminine)
  - **o sal** (salt - masculine)
  - Gender is not predictable - must memorize!

- **Partitives and quantities:**
  - um pedaço de pão (a piece of bread)
  - um copo de água (a glass of water)
  - uma xícara de café (a cup of coffee)
  - um prato de arroz (a plate of rice)
  - um pouco de sal (a little salt)

- **Brazilian staple: Arroz e feijão**
  - "Arroz **com** feijão" (rice and beans) - use COM (with)
  - This is THE staple of Brazilian cuisine, eaten daily
  - Often said as one phrase: "arroz e feijão"

### Exemplar sentences

- Eu gosto de arroz e feijão. (I like rice and beans.)
- Eu como frango com batata. (I eat chicken with potato.)
- Eu bebo suco de laranja. (I drink orange juice.)
- Eu quero um pedaço de pão. (I want a piece of bread.)
- Ela não come carne. (She doesn't eat meat.)
- Eu como frutas todos os dias. (I eat fruit every day.)
- Eu bebo água, não refrigerante. (I drink water, not soda.)

## Unit 72 — Transportation and Travel (Transporte e Viagem)

*Slug: `a2-transporte-viagem` · Sequence position: 65.0 · CEFR: A2 · Variant: shared*

**Concepts:** `directions`, `ir-transportation`

### Outcomes

- Name 11 modes of transportation
- Use correct preposition (de) with vehicles
- Use "a pé" correctly for walking
- Express how they get places: "Eu vou de carro"
- Talk about travel plans and destinations

### Vocabulary

- **Modes of transportation:**
  - o carro (car)
  - o ônibus (bus)
  - o metrô (subway/metro)
  - o trem (train)
  - o avião (airplane)
  - o táxi (taxi)
  - o Uber (Uber)
  - a bicicleta (bicycle)
  - a moto (motorcycle)
  - o barco (boat)
  - a pé (on foot)

- **Travel vocabulary:**
  - a viagem (trip/travel)
  - o aeroporto (airport)
  - a estação (station)
  - o bilhete (ticket)
  - a passagem (ticket - for travel)
  - a mala (suitcase)

### Grammar

- **Transportation prepositions - DE vs A PÉ:**
  - **de** + vehicle: "Eu vou **de** carro" (I go by car)
  - **de** ônibus, de metrô, de táxi, de avião, de trem, de bicicleta
  - **Exception: a pé** (on foot): "Eu vou **a pé**" (I go on foot)
  - NOT "de pé" - this is an exception!

- **IR (to go) + means of transportation:**
  - Eu vou de ônibus. (I go by bus.)
  - Eu vou de carro. (I go by car.)
  - Ele vai a pé. (He goes on foot.)
  - Structure: IR + de + transportation

- **PEGAR (to take/catch) + vehicle:**
  - Eu pego o ônibus. (I take/catch the bus.)
  - Eu pego o metrô. (I take the subway.)
  - "Pegar" means "to take/catch/get" a vehicle
  - Use definite article: pego **o** ônibus (not "pego ônibus")

- **Travel expressions with PARA:**
  - Eu vou **para** São Paulo. (I'm going to São Paulo.)
  - Eu viajo **para** o Brasil. (I'm traveling to Brazil.)
  - Use PARA (to/toward) for destination

### Exemplar sentences

- Eu vou de ônibus. (I go by bus.)
- Eu vou para o trabalho de carro. (I go to work by car.)
- Ela vai a pé. (She goes on foot.)
- Eu pego o metrô todos os dias. (I take the subway every day.)
- Eu viajo de avião. (I travel by plane.)
- Eu vou para São Paulo amanhã. (I'm going to São Paulo tomorrow.)
- Quanto custa a passagem de ônibus? (How much does the bus ticket cost?)

## Unit 73 — Hobbies and Leisure Activities (Hobbies e Atividades de Lazer)

*Slug: `a2-hobbies` · Sequence position: 66.0 · CEFR: A2 · Variant: shared*

**Concepts:** `hobbies`

### Outcomes

- Name 19 common hobbies and leisure activities
- Use JOGAR correctly for sports/games
- Use TOCAR correctly for instruments
- Express hobby preferences: "Eu gosto de ler"
- Combine hobbies with frequency adverbs

### Vocabulary

- **Sports and activities:**
  - jogar futebol (to play soccer)
  - jogar vôlei (to play volleyball)
  - jogar basquete (to play basketball)
  - nadar (to swim)
  - correr (to run)
  - caminhar (to walk/hike)
  - dançar (to dance)
  - cantar (to sing)

- **Leisure activities:**
  - ler (to read)
  - escrever (to write)
  - desenhar (to draw)
  - pintar (to paint)
  - tocar (to play instrument)
  - ouvir música (to listen to music)
  - assistir TV (to watch TV)
  - assistir filmes (to watch movies)
  - jogar videogame (to play video games)
  - viajar (to travel)
  - cozinhar (to cook)

### Grammar

- **JOGAR vs TOCAR - Critical distinction:**
  - **JOGAR** = play SPORTS/GAMES
    - jogar futebol (play soccer)
    - jogar vôlei (play volleyball)
    - jogar videogame (play video games)
    - jogar cartas (play cards)
  - **TOCAR** = play MUSICAL INSTRUMENTS
    - tocar violão (play guitar)
    - tocar piano (play piano)
    - tocar bateria (play drums)
  - **Do NOT confuse these two!**

- **GOSTAR DE + infinitive (to like to...):**
  - Eu gosto de ler. (I like to read.)
  - Ela gosta de nadar. (She likes to swim.)
  - Structure: gostar de + infinitive verb

- **Frequency with hobbies:**
  - Combining frequency adverbs (Unit 63) with hobbies:
  - Eu **sempre** jogo futebol. (I always play soccer.)
  - Eu **às vezes** leio. (I sometimes read.)

- **No article with sports after JOGAR:**
  - ✅ Eu jogo futebol. (I play soccer.) - NO article
  - ❌ Eu jogo o futebol. (wrong - don't use article)
  - Exception: specific game/match uses article
  - "Eu vou jogar o jogo" (I'm going to play the game - specific)

### Exemplar sentences

- Eu jogo futebol todo sábado. (I play soccer every Saturday.)
- Eu gosto de ler livros. (I like to read books.)
- Ela toca piano. (She plays piano.)
- Eu gosto de assistir filmes. (I like to watch movies.)
- Nós jogamos vôlei na praia. (We play volleyball on the beach.)
- Eu corro todos os dias. (I run every day.)
- Eu ouço música quando estudo. (I listen to music when I study.)

## Unit 74 — Technology and Communication (Tecnologia e Comunicação)

*Slug: `a2-tecnologia` · Sequence position: 67.0 · CEFR: A2 · Variant: shared*

**Concepts:** `technology`

### Outcomes

- Name 21 technology and communication terms
- Use LIGAR correctly (for calling and turning on)
- Use communication verbs (mandar, enviar, receber)
- Talk about technology use and habits
- Ask for WiFi password, phone numbers, etc.

### Vocabulary

- **Devices:**
  - o celular (cell phone)
  - o telefone (telephone)
  - o computador (computer)
  - o notebook (laptop)
  - o tablet (tablet)
  - a televisão / TV (television)
  - o relógio (watch/clock)

- **Communication:**
  - ligar (to call)
  - mandar mensagem (to send message)
  - enviar (to send)
  - receber (to receive)
  - responder (to respond/reply)
  - a mensagem (message)
  - o email (email)
  - o WhatsApp (WhatsApp)

- **Internet:**
  - a internet (internet)
  - o site (website)
  - o WiFi (WiFi)
  - a senha (password)
  - baixar (to download)
  - postar (to post)
  - o app / aplicativo (app)

### Grammar

- **Technology vocabulary often borrowed from English:**
  - WhatsApp, email, WiFi, site, app - same as English!
  - Pronounced with Portuguese accent but spelled similarly
  - Many tech terms are international

- **LIGAR (to call) - Multiple meanings:**
  - **ligar para** + person: "Eu ligo **para** você" (I call you)
  - **ligar** + device: "Eu ligo o computador" (I turn on the computer)
  - Same verb, different meanings based on context!
  - Use PARA when calling a person

- **MANDAR vs ENVIAR (both mean "to send"):**
  - **mandar** is more casual/common: "Eu mando uma mensagem"
  - **enviar** is more formal: "Eu envio um email"
  - Both are correct, mandar is more conversational

- **Using technology verbs:**
  - Eu **uso** o celular. (I use the cell phone.)
  - Eu **ligo** para minha mãe. (I call my mother.)
  - Eu **mando** mensagem. (I send a message.)
  - Eu **baixo** apps. (I download apps.)

### Exemplar sentences

- Eu uso o celular todos os dias. (I use my cell phone every day.)
- Eu ligo para minha família toda semana. (I call my family every week.)
- Eu mando mensagem no WhatsApp. (I send messages on WhatsApp.)
- Você tem WiFi? (Do you have WiFi?)
- Qual é a senha do WiFi? (What's the WiFi password?)
- Eu envio emails para o trabalho. (I send emails for work.)
- Eu baixo muitos apps. (I download many apps.)

## Unit 75 — Shopping and Money (Compras e Dinheiro)

*Slug: `a2-compras` · Sequence position: 68.0 · CEFR: A2 · Variant: shared*

**Concepts:** `shopping`

### Outcomes

- Name 21 shopping and money terms
- Use CUSTAR correctly (3rd person only)
- Ask and understand prices in reais
- Talk about payment methods (Pix, card, cash)
- Describe shopping experiences

### Vocabulary

- **Money:**
  - o dinheiro (money)
  - o real (Brazilian currency - singular)
  - os reais (Brazilian currency - plural)
  - a moeda (coin)
  - a nota (bill/banknote)
  - o cartão (card)
  - o cartão de crédito (credit card)
  - o cartão de débito (debit card)
  - o Pix (instant payment system)
  - o troco (change)

- **Shopping:**
  - a loja (store)
  - o mercado (market)
  - o supermercado (supermarket)
  - a farmácia (pharmacy)
  - comprar (to buy)
  - vender (to sell)
  - custar (to cost)
  - pagar (to pay)
  - o preço (price)
  - barato (cheap)
  - caro (expensive)

### Grammar

- **Brazilian currency: REAL/REAIS**
  - **Singular:** um real (R$ 1,00)
  - **Plural:** dois reais, três reais, cem reais
  - Written: R$ (símbolo do real)
  - R$ 10,00 = dez reais

- **CUSTAR (to cost) - special verb:**
  - **3rd person only** (like DOER in Unit 57)
  - Subject is the thing that costs, not the person!
  - **Singular:** custa (it costs)
  - **Plural:** custam (they cost)
  - Examples:
    - Quanto **custa**? (How much does it cost?)
    - **Custa** dez reais. (It costs ten reais.)
    - Os livros **custam** vinte reais. (The books cost twenty reais.)

- **PAGAR (to pay) - takes direct object OR por:**
  - Eu pago dez reais. (I pay ten reais.) - direct object
  - Eu pago **pelo** livro. (I pay for the book.) - por + o = pelo
  - Both structures are correct

- **PIX - Brazilian instant payment:**
  - Revolutionary payment system in Brazil (launched 2020)
  - Instant bank-to-bank transfer via phone
  - "Você aceita Pix?" (Do you accept Pix?)
  - "Eu faço um Pix" (I'll make a Pix payment)
  - Has largely replaced cash in Brazil!

### Exemplar sentences

- Quanto custa? (How much does it cost?)
- Custa dez reais. (It costs ten reais.)
- Eu pago com cartão. (I pay with card.)
- Você aceita Pix? (Do you accept Pix?)
- Isso é muito caro. (This is very expensive.)
- Eu compro no supermercado. (I buy at the supermarket.)
- Eu preciso de troco. (I need change.)

## Unit 76 — Professions and Work (Profissões e Trabalho)

*Slug: `a2-profissoes` · Sequence position: 69.0 · CEFR: A2 · Variant: shared*

**Concepts:** `work-professions`

### Outcomes

- Name 20+ common professions with correct gender
- Use SER + profession correctly (without article)
- Distinguish trabalhar EM (location) vs COMO (profession)
- Ask and answer about occupations
- Describe workplace and colleagues

### Vocabulary

- **Common professions:**
  - o médico / a médica (doctor)
  - o professor / a professora (teacher)
  - o enfermeiro / a enfermeira (nurse)
  - o engenheiro / a engenheira (engineer)
  - o advogado / a advogada (lawyer)
  - o dentista / a dentista (dentist - same form!)
  - o jornalista / a jornalista (journalist - same form!)
  - o estudante / a estudante (student - same form!)
  - o cozinheiro / a cozinheira (cook/chef)
  - o garçom / a garçonete (waiter/waitress)
  - o vendedor / a vendedora (salesperson)
  - o empresário / a empresária (businessperson)
  - o artista / a artista (artist - same form!)
  - o policial / a policial (police officer - same form!)

- **Work vocabulary:**
  - o trabalho (work/job)
  - a empresa (company)
  - o escritório (office)
  - o chefe / a chefe (boss)
  - o colega / a colega (colleague - same form!)
  - o salário (salary)

### Grammar

- **Gender agreement in professions:**
  - Most professions change -o to -a for feminine:
    - médico → médica
    - professor → professora
    - cozinheiro → cozinheira

  - Professions ending in -ista, -nte stay the SAME:
    - o dentista / a dentista (same word!)
    - o estudante / a estudante (same word!)
    - o artista / a artista (same word!)
    - Only the article changes!

- **Professions with unique feminine forms:**
  - o garçom / a garçonete (waiter/waitress - completely different)
  - o ator / a atriz (actor/actress - different forms)

- **Talking about professions - Two structures:**

  **Structure 1: SER + profession (no article):**
  - Eu sou médico. (I am a doctor.)
  - Ela é professora. (She is a teacher.)
  - NO article needed in Portuguese!

  **Structure 2: TRABALHAR COMO (work as):**
  - Eu trabalho como médico. (I work as a doctor.)
  - Ela trabalha como professora. (She works as a teacher.)

- **TRABALHAR EM (work at) vs TRABALHAR COMO (work as):**
  - **EM** = location: "Eu trabalho **em** um hospital" (I work at a hospital)
  - **COMO** = profession: "Eu trabalho **como** médico" (I work as a doctor)
  - Can combine: "Eu trabalho como médico em um hospital"

### Exemplar sentences

- Eu sou professor. (I am a teacher.)
- Ela é médica. (She is a doctor.)
- Eu trabalho como engenheiro. (I work as an engineer.)
- Eu trabalho em um hospital. (I work at a hospital.)
- Meu pai é advogado. (My father is a lawyer.)
- Ela trabalha como jornalista em São Paulo. (She works as a journalist in São Paulo.)
- O que você faz? - Eu sou dentista. (What do you do? - I'm a dentist.)

## Unit 77 — Health and Medical Basics (Saúde e Médico)

*Slug: `a2-saude` · Sequence position: 70.0 · CEFR: A2 · Variant: shared*

**Concepts:** `health-medical`, `body-parts`

### Outcomes

- Describe common health problems and symptoms
- Use ESTAR correctly for being sick
- Use TER for specific illnesses/symptoms
- Name medical places and professionals
- Ask for medicine and describe problems to doctor

### Vocabulary

- **Health conditions:**
  - doente (sick)
  - saudável (healthy)
  - a febre (fever)
  - a tosse (cough)
  - o resfriado (cold/flu)
  - a gripe (flu)
  - a dor (pain)
  - o remédio (medicine)
  - o comprimido (pill)
  - a receita (prescription)

- **Medical places:**
  - o hospital (hospital)
  - a clínica (clinic)
  - o consultório (doctor's office)
  - o posto de saúde (health center)
  - a farmácia (pharmacy)

- **Medical professionals (review + expand):**
  - o médico / a médica (doctor)
  - o enfermeiro / a enfermeira (nurse)
  - o dentista / a dentista (dentist)

### Grammar

- **ESTAR doente (to be sick) - uses ESTAR:**
  - Eu **estou** doente. (I am sick - temporary condition)
  - NOT "sou doente" - that would mean permanently sick!
  - Temporary health states always use ESTAR

- **TER (to have) with illnesses:**
  - Eu **tenho** febre. (I have a fever.)
  - Eu **tenho** tosse. (I have a cough.)
  - Eu **tenho** gripe. (I have the flu.)
  - Use TER (not ESTAR) for specific symptoms/illnesses

- **ESTAR COM (to be with) - alternative structure:**
  - Eu **estou com** febre. (I am with fever = I have a fever.)
  - Eu **estou com** dor de cabeça. (I have a headache.)
  - Both TER and ESTAR COM are correct!

- **Illness expressions:**
  - estar doente (to be sick)
  - estar bem (to be well)
  - estar mal (to feel bad/unwell)
  - ficar doente (to get/become sick)
  - melhorar (to get better)
  - piorar (to get worse)

### Exemplar sentences

- Eu estou doente. (I am sick.)
- Eu tenho febre. (I have a fever.)
- Eu estou com dor de cabeça. (I have a headache.)
- Eu preciso de um médico. (I need a doctor.)
- Eu vou à farmácia. (I'm going to the pharmacy.)
- Ela está com gripe. (She has the flu.)
- Eu preciso de remédio. (I need medicine.)

## Unit 78 — Commands/Imperative Mood (Imperativo)

*Slug: `a2-imperativo-bp` · Sequence position: 71.0 · CEFR: A2 · Variant: bp*

**Concepts:** `imperative-mood`

### Outcomes

- Give direct commands in Portuguese
- Form regular imperative (flip vowel rule)
- Use common irregular imperatives
- Make negative commands (não + imperative)
- Give polite instructions with "por favor"

### Vocabulary

- **Common command verbs:**
  - falar (to speak) → Fale! (Speak!)
  - comer (to eat) → Coma! (Eat!)
  - abrir (to open) → Abra! (Open!)
  - fechar (to close) → Feche! (Close!)
  - esperar (to wait) → Espere! (Wait!)
  - vir (to come) → Venha! (Come!)
  - ir (to go) → Vá! (Go!)
  - fazer (to do) → Faça! (Do!)
  - sentar (to sit) → Sente-se! (Sit down!)
  - levantar (to get up) → Levante-se! (Get up!)

### Grammar

- **Imperative mood - Commands:**
  - Used to give orders, instructions, requests
  - Different forms for você, vocês, and nós
  - This unit focuses on **você** form (most common)

- **Forming você commands:**

  **For -AR verbs:** Change -a to -e
  - falar → você fala → **Fale!** (Speak!)
  - comprar → você compra → **Compre!** (Buy!)
  - fechar → você fecha → **Feche!** (Close!)

  **For -ER/-IR verbs:** Change -e to -a
  - comer → você come → **Coma!** (Eat!)
  - abrir → você abre → **Abra!** (Open!)
  - escrever → você escreve → **Escreva!** (Write!)

- **Pattern: Flip the present tense vowel!**
  - -AR verbs: -a → -e
  - -ER/-IR verbs: -e → -a

- **Negative commands:**
  - Add **NÃO** before the verb:
  - **Não fale!** (Don't speak!)
  - **Não coma!** (Don't eat!)
  - **Não abra!** (Don't open!)

- **Common irregular imperatives:**
  - **ir** → **Vá!** (Go!)
  - **vir** → **Venha!** (Come!)
  - **fazer** → **Faça!** (Do!)
  - **ser** → **Seja!** (Be!)
  - **ter** → **Tenha!** (Have!)
  - **dar** → **Dê!** (Give!)
  - **estar** → **Esteja!** (Be!)

### Exemplar sentences

- Fale português! (Speak Portuguese!)
- Coma devagar! (Eat slowly!)
- Venha aqui! (Come here!)
- Vá para casa! (Go home!)
- Não fale alto! (Don't speak loudly!)
- Abra a porta, por favor. (Open the door, please.)
- Espere um momento! (Wait a moment!)

### Drills & artifacts

<!-- TODO: enrich in Phase 3 -->

## Unit 79 — Demonstratives - This/That (Demonstrativos)

*Slug: `a1-demonstrativos` · Sequence position: 72.0 · CEFR: A1 · Variant: shared*

**Concepts:** `demonstratives`

### Outcomes

- Use three-way demonstrative system correctly
- Choose este/esse/aquele based on distance
- Make demonstratives agree in gender and number
- Use demonstrative pronouns (este, aquele)
- Use neuter demonstratives (isto, isso, aquilo)

### Vocabulary

- **Demonstrative adjectives/pronouns:**
  - este/esta/estes/estas (this/these - near speaker)
  - esse/essa/esses/essas (that/those - near listener)
  - aquele/aquela/aqueles/aquelas (that/those - far from both)

- **Demonstrative pronouns (neuter):**
  - isto (this - abstract/general)
  - isso (that - abstract/general)
  - aquilo (that - abstract/general, far)

### Grammar

- **Three-way distinction in Portuguese:**

  Portuguese has THREE demonstratives, not two like English!

  **ESTE (this) - near the speaker:**
  - **Este** livro (this book - in my hand)
  - Near me, the person speaking
  - Equivalent to "this" in English

  **ESSE (that) - near the listener:**
  - **Esse** livro (that book - in your hand)
  - Near you, the person listening
  - Equivalent to "that" in English (near)

  **AQUELE (that) - far from both:**
  - **Aquele** livro (that book - over there)
  - Far from both speaker and listener
  - Equivalent to "that over there" in English

- **Gender and number agreement:**

  Demonstratives MUST agree with the noun:

  **Masculine singular:**
  - este livro (this book)
  - esse carro (that car)
  - aquele homem (that man over there)

  **Feminine singular:**
  - esta casa (this house)
  - essa mulher (that woman)
  - aquela loja (that store over there)

  **Masculine plural:**
  - estes livros (these books)
  - esses carros (those cars)
  - aqueles homens (those men over there)

  **Feminine plural:**
  - estas casas (these houses)
  - essas mulheres (those women)
  - aquelas lojas (those stores over there)

- **Demonstrative pronouns (replacing nouns):**
  - Eu quero **este**. (I want this one.)
  - Eu prefiro **aquele**. (I prefer that one over there.)
  - **Estas** são minhas. (These are mine.)

- **Neuter demonstratives (for abstract things):**
  - **Isto** é importante. (This is important.)
  - **Isso** é verdade. (That is true.)
  - **Aquilo** é estranho. (That is strange.)
  - Use when NOT referring to specific noun

### Exemplar sentences

- Este livro é meu. (This book is mine - I have it)
- Esse livro é seu? (Is that book yours? - you have it)
- Aquele livro é caro. (That book is expensive - over there)
- Eu quero esta camisa. (I want this shirt.)
- Você gosta desses sapatos? (Do you like those shoes? - pointing to listener)
- Aquelas casas são grandes. (Those houses are big - over there)
- Isto é importante. (This is important.)

## Unit 80 — Furniture and Household Items (Móveis e Objetos da Casa)

*Slug: `a1-moveis` · Sequence position: 73.0 · CEFR: A1 · Variant: shared*

**Concepts:** `house-rooms`

### Outcomes

- Name 24+ common furniture and household items
- Use TER to describe what's in rooms
- Describe where furniture is located
- Use adjectives with furniture
- Describe their home in detail

### Vocabulary

- **Living room furniture:**
  - o sofá (sofa/couch)
  - a poltrona (armchair)
  - a mesa de centro (coffee table)
  - a estante (bookshelf)
  - a televisão (television)
  - o tapete (rug/carpet)

- **Bedroom furniture:**
  - a cama (bed)
  - o guarda-roupa (wardrobe/closet)
  - o travesseiro (pillow)
  - o cobertor (blanket)
  - o lençol (sheet)

- **Kitchen items:**
  - a geladeira (refrigerator)
  - o fogão (stove)
  - o micro-ondas (microwave)
  - a pia (sink)
  - a mesa (table)
  - a cadeira (chair)

- **Bathroom items:**
  - o chuveiro (shower)
  - a pia (sink)
  - o vaso sanitário (toilet)
  - o espelho (mirror)
  - a toalha (towel)

### Grammar

- **TER (to have) with furniture:**
  - Na sala **tem** um sofá. (In the living room there is a sofa.)
  - Meu quarto **tem** uma cama grande. (My room has a big bed.)
  - Using TER for "there is/there are" in rooms

- **Prepositions with furniture:**
  - **em cima da** mesa (on top of the table)
  - **embaixo da** cama (under the bed)
  - **ao lado do** sofá (next to the sofa)
  - **na** estante (in/on the bookshelf)

- **Describing furniture:**
  - sofá grande (big sofa)
  - cama confortável (comfortable bed)
  - mesa pequena (small table)
  - Adjectives agree with furniture gender/number

### Exemplar sentences

- Na sala tem um sofá. (In the living room there's a sofa.)
- Meu quarto tem uma cama grande. (My room has a big bed.)
- A geladeira está na cozinha. (The refrigerator is in the kitchen.)
- O livro está em cima da mesa. (The book is on top of the table.)
- Eu preciso de uma cadeira. (I need a chair.)
- O espelho está no banheiro. (The mirror is in the bathroom.)
- Meu sofá é muito confortável. (My sofa is very comfortable.)

## Unit 81 — Nature and Animals (Natureza e Animais)

*Slug: `a2-natureza-animais` · Sequence position: 74.0 · CEFR: A2 · Variant: shared*

**Concepts:** `common-expressions`

### Outcomes

- Name 10+ common animals
- Name 14+ nature vocabulary items
- Talk about pets using TER
- Describe natural environments
- Use nature vocabulary with prepositions

### Vocabulary

- **Common animals:**
  - o cachorro (dog)
  - o gato (cat)
  - o pássaro (bird)
  - o peixe (fish)
  - o cavalo (horse)
  - a vaca (cow)
  - o porco (pig)
  - a galinha (chicken)
  - o coelho (rabbit)
  - o rato (rat/mouse)

- **Nature vocabulary:**
  - a árvore (tree)
  - a flor (flower)
  - a planta (plant)
  - a grama (grass)
  - a montanha (mountain)
  - o rio (river)
  - o lago (lake)
  - o mar (sea)
  - a praia (beach)
  - a floresta (forest)
  - o céu (sky)
  - o sol (sun)
  - a lua (moon)
  - a estrela (star)

### Grammar

- **TER (to have) with pets:**
  - Eu **tenho** um cachorro. (I have a dog.)
  - Você **tem** animais? (Do you have animals/pets?)
  - Structure: TER + animal

- **Animals with gender variations:**
  - **o cachorro / a cachorra** (male dog / female dog)
  - **o gato / a gata** (male cat / female cat)
  - But often use masculine for generic: "Eu tenho um cachorro" (I have a dog - could be male or female)

- **Nature with prepositions:**
  - **na** praia (at/on the beach)
  - **no** rio (in the river)
  - **na** montanha (in/on the mountain)
  - **na** floresta (in the forest)

- **Describing animals:**
  - cachorro grande (big dog)
  - gato preto (black cat)
  - pássaro pequeno (small bird)
  - Adjectives agree with animal gender

### Exemplar sentences

- Eu tenho um cachorro. (I have a dog.)
- Meu gato é preto. (My cat is black.)
- O pássaro está na árvore. (The bird is in the tree.)
- Eu gosto de ir à praia. (I like to go to the beach.)
- A montanha é alta. (The mountain is tall.)
- Tem muitas flores no jardim. (There are many flowers in the garden.)
- O rio é grande. (The river is big.)
